/bin/bash -lc "env OPENBLAS_NUM_THREADS=1 OMP_NUM_THREADS=1 MKL_NUM_THREADS=1 python3 -u - <<'PY'
import csv,sys,importlib.util
from pathlib import Path
import numpy as np
from scipy.integrate import solve_ivp
root=Path('/tmp/udt_global_assembly_verifier.w1qTCB')
pkg=root/'udt_global_metric_assembly_atlas_2026-07-22'
spec=importlib.util.spec_from_file_location('v',pkg/'verify_global_assembly_atlas.py');v=importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec);spec.loader.exec_module(v)
rows=list(csv.DictReader(open(pkg/'DENSE_TRANSPORT_ATLAS.tsv'),delimiter='\\t'))
idmap={r['identity_id']:r for r in v.frozen.identities()}; fmap={r['family_id']:r for r in v.frozen.FAMILIES}
worst_i=(-1,None);worst_m=(-1,None);fails=[]
for idx,row in enumerate(rows,1):
 identity=idmap[row['identity_id']];family=fmap[row['family_id']]
 def rhs(t,flat): return (v.independent_generator(identity,family,float(t))[0]@flat.reshape(4,4)).reshape(-1)

   609	def monodromy_registry() -> list[dict[str, object]]:
   610	    witnesses = {
   611	        "M_IDENTITY": [[1, 0], [0, 1]],
   612	        "M_MINUS_IDENTITY": [[-1, 0], [0, -1]],
   613	        "M_ORDER4_ROTATION": [[0, -1], [1, 0]],
   614	        "M_ORDER6_ELLIPTIC": [[0, -1], [1, 1]],
   615	        "M_PARABOLIC": [[1, 1], [0, 1]],
   616	        "M_HYPERBOLIC": [[2, 1], [1, 1]],
   617	        "M_EXCHANGE": [[0, 1], [1, 0]],
   618	        "M_ORIENTATION_REVERSING_GLIDE": [[1, 1], [0, -1]],
   619	    }
   620	    rows = []
   621	    for name, values in witnesses.items():
   622	        matrix = np.asarray(values, dtype=int)
   623	        det = int(round(np.linalg.det(matrix)))
   624	        trace = int(np.trace(matrix))
   625	        if det == -1:
   626	            kind = "ORIENTATION_REVERSING"
   627	        elif matrix.tolist() == [[1, 0], [0, 1]]:
   628	            kind = "IDENTITY"
   629	        elif abs(trace) < 2:
   630	            kind = "FINITE_ELLIPTIC"
   631	        elif abs(trace) == 2:
   632	            kind = "PARABOLIC_OR_MINUS_PARABOLIC"
   633	        else:
   634	            kind = "HYPERBOLIC"
   635	        coker = abelian_coker(matrix - np.eye(2, dtype=int))
   636	        rows.append({
   637	            "monodromy_id": name,
   638	            "matrix": json.dumps(values, separators=(",", ":")),
   639	            "determinant": det,
   640	            "trace": trace,
   641	            "monodromy_class": kind,
   642	            "fiber_coker_M_minus_I": coker,
   643	            "mapping_torus_H1": f"Z+({coker})",
   644	            "coverage_status": "PARAMETRIC_GL2Z_FAMILY_WITH_CLASS_WITNESS",
   645	        })
   646	    return rows

--- frozen CSN consequence ---
   236	## What the registered UDT selectors actually do
   237	
   238	### Reciprocity
   239	
   240	Reciprocity supplies the determinant-one exponential comparison pair. Within the Hopf-coordinate
   241	witness, `phi -> -phi` exchanges the two orbit scale factors. It does not universally duplicate or
   242	reassign the founding temporal/parallel pair into a transverse spatial torus, declare those
   243	directions periodic, or specify their collapse lattice.
   244	
   245	### Common-Scale Neutrality
   246	
   247	CSN removes a positive common factor from the interior orbit block and from the normalized
   248	metric-dual connection. At a genuine cap, an orbit coefficient or determinant representative
   249	degenerates. Smooth cap completion is additional global/boundary information, not a positive CSN
   250	gauge transformation through zero.
   251	
   252	### Finite-cell structure
   253	
   254	The binding canon fixes a monotone finite domain terminated by a physical mirrored boundary/fold,
   255	with no spatial infinity. Within that setting, its only toric-relevant field datum is the static
   256	`phi` condition: `phi` is odd at the seal, its value is zero, and its normal derivative remains free.
   257	It expressly does not select the boundary functional or the boundary data of other fields. It says
   258	nothing about a transverse torus lattice, angular exchange, endpoint collapse cycles, or a quotient
   259	action.
   260	
   261	### Bootstrap
   262	
   263	The current bootstrap principle says the realized matter-bearing universe must be a complete
   264	self-consistent global solution in a narrow total-density window. The full time-live volume,
   265	physical boundary, equations, action, and stability gates remain open. The bootstrap-variation audit
   266	also finds no off-shell representative-selection or matching map. There is therefore no registered
   267	operator that compares and ranks `T3`, `S3`, lens, boundary-cylinder, round, or non-round closures.
   268	
   269	Bootstrap could eventually select among complete solutions after that missing law exists. It cannot
   270	presently be used as the missing law itself.
